    document.addEventListener('wpdg:socket:event', function (e) {
      const { eventName, payload } = e.detail || {};
      const h = window.WPDG_SOCKET_HANDLERS || {};
      if (typeof h[eventName] === 'function') h[eventName](payload);
    });

<script>
/**
 * Filtri & interazioni UI (sempre attivi)
 * - Toggle via classi (più veloce di style.display)
 * - Messaggio "nessuna partita" gestito in modo idempotente
 */
(function () {
  // Stato iniziale filtro
  let currentFilter = 'all';
  window.currentFilter = currentFilter; // esposto per altri script

  const HIDDEN_CLASS = 'dg-hidden';

  // Aggiungi regola CSS per nascondere (se non già presente)
  function ensureHiddenCss() {
    if (document.getElementById('dg-hidden-style')) return;
    const s = document.createElement('style');
    s.id = 'dg-hidden-style';
    s.textContent = `.dg-hidden{display:none!important}`;
    document.head.appendChild(s);
  }

  // Messaggio "nessuna partita"
  function ensureNoMatchesMsg(container) {
    let msg = container.querySelector('.no-matches-message');
    if (!msg) {
      msg = document.createElement('div');
      msg.className = 'no-matches-message';
      msg.style.cssText = 'margin:150px auto;text-align:center';
      msg.innerHTML = '<i class="fa-regular fa-hand" style="color:#666;font-size:4rem"></i><br/><br/><span style="color:#666;font-size:1.1rem;font-weight:bold">Nessuna partita da visualizzare</span>';
      container.appendChild(msg);
    }
    return msg;
  }

  // Funzione principale filtro
  function filterMatches(filter) {
    window.currentFilter = currentFilter = filter;

    // Aggiorna URL senza ricaricare
    const url = new URL(window.location);
    (filter === 'all') ? url.searchParams.delete('filter') : url.searchParams.set('filter', filter);
    window.history.pushState({}, '', url);

    // Aggiorna tabs
    document.querySelectorAll('.dg-tabs ul li').forEach(tab => {
      tab.classList.toggle('active', tab.getAttribute('data-filter') === filter);
    });

    const container = document.getElementById('tournaments-container');
    if (!container) return;

    const tournaments = container.querySelectorAll('.dg-tournament');
    let visibleCount = 0;

    tournaments.forEach(tournament => {
      const matches = tournament.querySelectorAll('.dg-tournament-row');
      const body = tournament.querySelector('.dg-tournament-body');
      let hasVisible = false;

      matches.forEach(match => {
        const status = match.dataset.status;                // es: 'live' | 'closed' | ...
        const isFav  = match.dataset.isFavourite === '1';
        let show = true;

        switch (filter) {
          case 'live':       show = (status === 'inprogress');   break;
          case 'closed':     show = (status === 'finished'); break;
          case 'favourites': show = isFav;                 break;
          default:           show = true;
        }

        match.classList.toggle(HIDDEN_CLASS, !show);
        if (show) { hasVisible = true; visibleCount++; }
      });

      // Mostra torneo solo se contiene partite visibili
      tournament.classList.toggle(HIDDEN_CLASS, !hasVisible);

      // Con filtro "live" mantieni espanso
      if (hasVisible && filter === 'live' && body) {
        body.classList.remove('hidden');
      }
    });

    // Messaggio se nessuna partita visibile
    const existingMsg = container.querySelector('.no-matches-message');
    if (visibleCount === 0) {
      ensureNoMatchesMsg(container);
    } else if (existingMsg) {
      existingMsg.remove();
    }
  }


  // Init
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
    ensureHiddenCss();
    if (currentFilter !== 'all') {
      // Applica filtro iniziale se richiesto da query string
      filterMatches(currentFilter);
    }
  });

  // Esporta global
  window.filterMatches = filterMatches;
})();
</script>

<script>
(function() {
  var SHOW_DELAY_MS = 800;
  var STORAGE_KEY   = "dg_app_popup_suppressed_until";
  var SUPPRESS_DAYS = 1;

  if (!window.matchMedia || !window.matchMedia("(max-width: 768px)").matches) return;
  try {
    var until = localStorage.getItem(STORAGE_KEY);
    if (until && Date.now() < Number(until)) return;
  } catch(e){}

  var ua = navigator.userAgent || "";
  var isAndroid = /Android/i.test(ua);
  var isIOS     = /iPhone|iPad|iPod/i.test(ua);

  var link, btnText, btnClass;
  if (isIOS) {
    link     = "https://qrurl.it/pYBEv";
    btnText  = "Scarica su App Store";
    btnClass = "ios";
  } else {
    link     = "https://qrurl.it/wL1gv";
    btnText  = "Scarica su Google Play";
    btnClass = "android";
  }

  var overlay = document.getElementById("dg-app-overlay");
  var popup   = document.getElementById("dg-app-popup");
  var closeBtn= document.getElementById("dg-close");
  var linkEl  = document.getElementById("dg-link");

  linkEl.href = link;
  linkEl.textContent = btnText;
  linkEl.classList.add(btnClass);

  function openPopup() {
    overlay.style.display = "block";
    popup.style.display   = "block";
  }
  function closePopup() {
    popup.style.display   = "none";
    overlay.style.display = "none";
    try {
      var untilTs = Date.now() + SUPPRESS_DAYS*24*60*60*1000;
      localStorage.setItem(STORAGE_KEY, String(untilTs));
    } catch(e){}
  }

  overlay.addEventListener("click", closePopup);
  closeBtn.addEventListener("click", closePopup);

  setTimeout(openPopup, SHOW_DELAY_MS);
})();
</script>

    var t;
    window.onload = dadaResetTime;
    window.onmousemove = dadaResetTime;
